 Philosopher, economist, sociologist and revolutionary socialist Karl Marx was born on 5 May 1818
 jaaniye is samyavaadee purodha ke bare main mahatvapurn jaankaree
 
 
 1
 wo taumr kaamkaaji tabake kii aawaaj buland karte rahe
 Due to this they also had to face a lot of opposition from the bourgeoisie
 2
 Together with Frederick Engels, he created 'the Communist Manifesto'
 isamen samyawad kii avdhaaran pesh kii gai he
 3
 apane krantikari lekhon ke kaaran unhen germany, france or belgium se bhaga diya gaya tha
 4
 marks kii pankti 'duniya ke mazdooron ke paalpani zanjeerake alaava khone ke liye kuch bhi nahin he, duniya ke mazdooron ek ho' aaj bhi duniya ke har majdoor andolan kaa naaraa he
 5
 1864 main landan main 'antarrashtriya majdoor sangh' kii sthapana main marks ne bahut mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaai
 6
 saal 1867 main unhone das capital kaa pehla wolum chapa, jo unki aarthikvichaardharaka byoraa he
 The remaining part of 'das Capital' was edited and published by Engels after Marx's death
 7
 The theory of 'class struggle' is the backbone of Marx's 'scientific socialism'

 1

 iske saath hi arabiai ne ye bhi anumati de di he ki sabhi bank jamaa sone par khud byaaj daren tay kar sakate hai
 4) Gold check before depositing: In this scheme, gold can be deposited in three ways
 short turm (1 se 3 saal), medium turm (5 se 7 saal) or long turm (12 se 15 saal)
 Also, before depositing the gold, its purity will be checked
 iske baad hi jamaa karne sambandhi kaam aage badhaayaa ja sakegaa
